靜態網頁擷取¶

郭耀仁¶

先安裝兩個 chrome 外掛¶

  • SelectorGadget: 幫助 CSS 選擇
  • XPath Helper: 幫助 XPath 選擇

CSS 選擇¶

  • 利用文件物件模型（Document Object Model, DOM）選擇網頁元素的技巧

CSS 選擇（2）¶

  • 以 IMDB: La La Land 為例
  • 選出評等（Rating）

CSS 選擇（3）¶

  • 點選 SelectorGadget 的外掛圖示
  • 先點選評等（Rating）

CSS 選擇（4）¶

  • 會有多個元素被選出（標註黃色），因為這頁有很多 <span></span>

CSS 選擇（5）¶

  • 接著點選不要的元素（標註紅色）

CSS 選擇（6）¶

  • 這時我們就得到正確的 CSS 選擇：strong span

CSS 選擇（7）¶

  • 再練習一次，這次我們要將這頁的演員名單（Cast）擷取出來：

CSS 選擇（8）¶

  • 先點選男主角 Ryan Gosling
  • 乍看之下好像 .itemprop 這個類別就對了

CSS 選擇（9）¶

  • 但是其實其他的元素也有使用 .itemprop 這個類別

CSS 選擇（10）¶

  • 於是點選不要的元素（標註紅色）

CSS 選擇（11）¶

  • 這時我們就得到正確的 CSS 選擇：.itemprop .itemprop

XPath 選擇¶

  • 點選 XPath Helper 外掛圖示
  • 按住 shift 之後將游標移到評等（Rating）上面

XPath 選擇（2）¶

  • 試著將 XPath 縮短一點，可以得到 XPath 選擇：//strong/span

XPath 選擇（3）¶

  • 再練習一次，這次我們要將這頁的演員名單（Cast）擷取出來：

XPath 選擇（4）¶

  • 按住 shift 後點選男主角 Ryan Gosling

XPath 選擇（5）¶

  • 按住 shift 後點選女主角 Emma Stone

XPath 選擇（6）¶

  • 再點選幾個演員之後會發現 /tbody/tr[@class='even'] 跟 /tbody/tr[@class='odd'] 一直在變更
  • 試著將變更的部分都刪除掉，得到我們要的 XPath 選擇：//td[@class='itemprop']/a/span[@class='itemprop']

Beautiful Soup¶

  • 用來解析 HTML 與 XML 檔案的 Python 模組
  • 先在終端機安裝模組
pip install beautifulsoup4
In [1]:
import urllib.request

lalaland_url = "http://www.imdb.com/title/tt3783958/"
f = urllib.request.urlopen(lalaland_url)
html_doc = f.read()

    <div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">\n            <p>\nAspiring actress serves lattes to movie stars in between auditions and jazz musician Sebastian scrapes by playing cocktail-party gigs in dingy bars. But as success mounts, they are faced with decisions that fray the fragile fabric of their love affair, and the dreams they worked so hard to maintain in each other threaten to rip them apart.                <em class="nobr">Written by\n<a href="/search/title?plot_author=Eirini&view=simple&sort=alpha&ref_=tt_stry_pl"\n>Eirini</a></em>            </p>\n        </div>\n        \n        <span   \n    \n    \n\n    <div class="article" id="titleFAQ">\n        <h2>Frequently Asked Questions</h2>\n<a href="/title/tt3783958/faq?ref_=tt_faq_sm"\n>This FAQ is empty. Add the first question.</a> \n    </div>    \n\n\n    \n    \n    \n\n\n\n<script>\n    if (typeof uet == \'function\') {\n      uet("bb", "TitleUserReviewsWidget", {wb: 1});\n    }\n</script>\n  <script>\n    if (\'csm\' in window) {\n      csm.measure(\'csm_TitleUserReviewsWidget_started\');\n    }\n  </script>\n    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">\n        <h2>User Reviews</h2>\n        <div class="user-comments">\n                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="10/10">\n                        <div style="width: 100px;">&nbsp;</div>\n                    </div>\n                <span itemprop="review" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">  \n                    <strong itemprop="name">Love letter to Hollywood .. and a Heck of a Film</strong>\n                        <span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">\n                            <meta itemprop="worstRating" content = "1" />\n                            <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="10" />\n                            <meta itemprop="bestRating" content="10" />\n                        </span>\n                    <div class="comment-meta">\n                        1 January 2017 | by <a href="/user/ur44112735/?ref_=tt_urv"\n><span itemprop="author">A_Different_Drummer</span></a>\n                        <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-01-01" />\n                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur44112735/comments?ref_=tt_urv"\n>See all my reviews</a>\n                    </div>\n                    <div>\n                        <p itemprop="reviewBody">Writer/Director Damien Chazelle, who already had a nice career going for him, explodes into the Bigtime with this delightful, mesmerizing, and completely unexpected ode to Tinseltown.<br/><br/>The opening sequence (satirized on the Golden Globes) really does not do the rest of the film justice. It is as if the cast from the FAME remake grew up, had children of their own, and then those children hijacked the Santa Monica freeway to do a 10 minute flash-mob dance sequence.<br/><br/>From that point on, the film is hypnotic.<br/><br/>We segue to a love story as pure as anything since the great dramas of the 1940s. If the film had been in B&amp;W, you would almost have expected to see Bette Davis in a 3-hankie tear jerker.<br/><br/>Except for the musical interludes, of course, which are pitch perfect and totally wonderful.<br/><br/>Gosling is surprising as a leading man expected to do song and dance, but he delivers the goods. <br/><br/>Stone, who was supposed to be &quot;the next big thing&quot; after Easy A (2010), steals the film and possibly the hearts of the audience as well. The awards should flow like water, and she will deserve every one.<br/><br/>As I said, deep in the DNA this is an ode to Hollywood. The film industry has always had issues with endings -- back in the day they would film several different endings per picture -- and then decide at the last minute which to use. Here Chazelle pays homage to that by giving us an alternate ending, along with the &quot;real&quot; ending, along with a closing sequence designed to remind everyone that nothing in Hollywood is actually real, but everything still can be really fun.<br/><br/>Destined to be a classic. Recommended.</p>\n                    </div>\n                </span>\n                <hr />\n\n\n                <div class="yn" id="ynd_rw3610731">\n                463 of 830 people found this    <div class="article" id="titleStoryLine">
    <span class="rightcornerlink">
     <a href="/register/login?why=edit&amp;ref_=tt_stry" rel="login">
      Edit
     </a>
    </span>
    <h2>
     Storyline
    </h2>
    <div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
     <p>
      Aspiring actress serves lattes to movie stars in between auditions and jazz musician Sebastian scrapes by playing cocktail-party gigs in dingy bars. But as success mounts, they are faced with decisions that fray the fragile fabric of their love affair, and the dreams they worked so hard to maintain in each other threaten to rip them apart.
      <em class="nobr">
       Written by
       <a href="/search/title?plot_author=Eirini&amp;view=simple&amp;sort=alpha&amp;ref_=tt_stry_pl">
        Eirini
       </a>
      </em>
     </p>
    </div>

   <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
    <h2>
     User Reviews
    </h2>
    <div class="user-comments">
     <div class="tinystarbar" title="10/10">
      <div style="width: 100px;">
      </div>
     </div>
     <span itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
      <strong itemprop="name">
       Love letter to Hollywood .. and a Heck of a Film
      </strong>
      <span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
       <meta content="1" itemprop="worstRating"/>
       <meta content="10" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
       <meta content="10" itemprop="bestRating"/>
      </span>
      <div class="comment-meta">
       1 January 2017 | by
       <a href="/user/ur44112735/?ref_=tt_urv">
        <span itemprop="author">
         A_Different_Drummer
        </span>
       </a>
       <meta content="2017-01-01" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       –
       <a href="/user/ur44112735/comments?ref_=tt_urv">
        See all my reviews
       </a>
      </div>
      <div>
       <p itemprop="reviewBody">
        Writer/Director Damien Chazelle, who already had a nice career going for him, explodes into the Bigtime with this delightful, mesmerizing, and completely unexpected ode to Tinseltown.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        The opening sequence (satirized on the Golden Globes) really does not do the rest of the film justice. It is as if the cast from the FAME remake grew up, had children of their own, and then those children hijacked the Santa Monica freeway to do a 10 minute flash-mob dance sequence.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        From that point on, the film is hypnotic.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        We segue to a love story as pure as anything since the great dramas of the 1940s. If the film had been in B&amp;W, you would almost have expected to see Bette Davis in a 3-hankie tear jerker.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Except for the musical interludes, of course, which are pitch perfect and totally wonderful.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Gosling is surprising as a leading man expected to do song and dance, but he delivers the goods.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Stone, who was supposed to be "the next big thing" after Easy A (2010), steals the film and possibly the hearts of the audience as well. The awards should flow like water, and she will deserve every one.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        As I said, deep in the DNA this is an ode to Hollywood. The film industry has always had issues with endings -- back in the day they would film several different endings per picture -- and then decide at the last minute which to use. Here Chazelle pays homage to that by giving us an alternate ending, along with the "real" ending, along with a closing sequence designed to remind everyone that nothing in Hollywood is actually real, but everything still can be really fun.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Destined to be a classic. Recommended.
       </p>
      </div>
     </span>
     <hr/>

                jQuery(
                             function() {
            var facebookTheme = (window.custom && window.custom.full_page &&
                    window.custom.full_page.theme) ?
                window.custom.full_page.theme : "light",
            url = "//www.facebook.com/plugins/likebox.php?href=facebook.com%2Fimdb&width=300&height=190&connections=4&header=false&stream=false&colorscheme=" + facebookTheme,
            like = document.getElementById('facebookIframe'),
            twitterIframe = document.getElementById('twitterIframe');
            if (like) {
                like.src = url;
            }
            if (twitterIframe) {
                twitterIframe.src = "http://ia.media-imdb.com/images/G/01/imdb/html/twitter-follow-4260519736._CB491967851_.html?10#imdb";
            }
         }

                );
            } else if (remaining_count > 0) {
                setTimeout(function() { jQueryOnReady(remaining_count-1) }, 100);
            }
        }
        jQueryOnReady(50);
</script>

BeautifulSoup 的缺點¶

  • 對 CSS 選擇的支援有限
  • 沒有對 XPath 選擇支援
  • 必須搭配 urllib.request.urlopen()
  • 無法解決動態網頁問題，e.g. 如果要在 IMDB 搜尋電影名稱再進行擷取
